Credits A Note Authors: Brian Campbell (Black Spiral Dancers), Sam We confess: As foul as this book may be, it could Inabinet (Cosmology), Deena McKinney (Pentex), Jim be a lot fouler. In many cases, we’ve opted to leave the Moore (Monsters) full extent of the Wyrm’s particular depravities to your A Additional Material: Justin Achilli, Echan Skemp imagination. There’s really two reasons. Developer: Ethan Skemp The first is pretty simple: using your imagination Editor: Aileen E. Miles to fill in the blanks creates things that are much more Art Director: Aileen E. Miles personal and effective than we might be able to manLayout & Typesetting: Pauline Benney age. You know what scares you most, so you know what Art: Andrew Bates, Ron Brown, John Cobb, themes to emphasize for maximum horror. This book's Guy Davis, Steve Ellis, Jeff Holt, Brian LeBlanc, | 4 blueprint — not a house. You get to hang the Vince Locke, Steve Prescott, Ron Spencer, James Stowe, paintings to your taste. Joshua Gabriel Timbrook The second reason's fairly simple, too. AdmitCover Art: Ron Spencer tedly, if we wanted to be thorough, this book could Cover Design: Pauline Benney easily be Black Dog, shrinkwrapped, and only sold to people 35 and older who are wearing gloves. However, it’s up to the individual to determine just how much of the Wyrm's spiritual corruption should be graphically visible in the average story. You might find it appropriate to have the Black Spiral Dancers carry the captured characters back to the Hive, gang-rape them, flay them and feed them to a Thunderwyrm — and describe the whole process — but that kind of shock value can quickly turn the game into absolutely no fun ar all, depending on the participants’ morés. Werewolf is at heart a game — entertainment — and if your players feel that certain scenes are inappropriate and more disturbing than entertaining, that’s their right. Use your discretion. © 1998 White Wolf Publishing, Inc. Background: The Inquisitors are an unknown quantity in the equations of the Triat. Everything about them suggests they belong to the Weaver, but they are very heavily tainted by the Wyrm. Pentex is very interested in them, and desperately wants to know who is behind these faceless creatures. So far they've managed to locate and torture over 50 Pentex agents, at least seven Garou and one Corax. Whatever their agenda might be, they've yet to reveal it to anyone.
